LINE# LOC   CODE        LINE


01842  EEBB              ; RSTRAB - ENTRY FOR NMI CONTINUE ROUTINE
01843  EEBB              ; RSTBGN - ENTRY FOR START TRANSMITTER
01844  EEBB              ;
01845  EEBB              ;   RSR - 8/18/80
01846  EEBB              ;
01847  EEBB              ; VARIABLES USED
01848  EEBB              ;   BITTS - # OF BITS TO BE SENT (<>0 NOT DONE)
01849  EEBB              ;   NXTBIT - BYTE CONTAINS NEXT BIT TO BE SENT
01850  EEBB              ;   ROPRTY - BYTE CONTAINS PARITY BIT CALCULATED
01851  EEBB              ;   RODATA - STORES DATA BYTE CURRENTLY BEING TRANSMITTED
01852  EEBB              ;   RODBS - OUTPUT BUFFER INDEX START
01853  EEBB              ;   RODBE - OUTPUT BUFFER INDEX END
01854  EEBB              ;   IF RODBS=RODBE THEN BUFFER EMPTY
01855  EEBB              ;   ROBUF - INDIRECT POINTER TO DATA BUFFER
01856  EEBB              ;   RSSTAT - RS-232 STATUS BYTE
01857  EEBB              ;
01858  EEBB              ;   XXX US - NORMAL BIT PATH
01859  EEBB              ;   XXX US - WORST CASE PARITY BIT PATH
01860  EEBB              ;   XXX US - STOP BIT PATH
01861  EEBB              ;   XXX US - START BIT PATH
01862  EEBB              ;
01863  EEBB  A5 B4       RSTRAB LDA BITTS       ;CHECK FOR PLACE IN BYTE...
01864  EEBD  F0 47              BEQ RSTBGN      ;...DONE, =0 START NEXT
01865  EEBF              ;
01866  EEBF  30 3F              BMI RST050      ;...DOING STOP BITS
01867  EEC1              ;
01868  EEC1  46 B6              LSR RODATA      ;SHIFT DATA INTO CARRY
01869  EEC3  A2 00              LDX #00         ;PREPARE FOR A ZERO
01870  EEC5  90 01              BCC RST005      ;YES...A ZERO
01871  EEC7  CA                 DEX             ;NO...MAKE AN $FF
01872  EEC8  8A          RST005 TXA             ;READY TO SEND
01873  EEC9              ;
01874  EEC9  45 BD              EOR ROPRTY      ;CALC INTO PARITY
01875  EECB  85 BD              STA ROPRTY
01876  EECD              ;
01877  EECD  C6 B4              DEC BITTS       ;BIT COUNT DOWN
01878  EECF  F0 06              BEQ RST010      ;WANT A PARITY INSTEAD
01879  EED1              ;
01880  EED1  8A          RSTEXT TXA             ;CALC BIT WHOLE TO SEND
01881  EED2  29 04              AND #$04        ;GOES OUT D2PA2
01882  EED4  85 B5              STA NXTBIT
01883  EED6  60                 RTS

01885  EED7              ; CALCULATE PARITY

01887  EED7              ;

01983  EF59              ; RSRCVR - NMI ROUTINE TO COLLECT
01984  EF59              ;  DATA INTO BYTES
01985  EF59              ;
01986  EF59              ; RSR 8/18/80
01987  EF59              ;
01988  EF59              ; VARIABLES USED
01989  EF59              ;   INBIT - INPUT BIT VALUE
01990  EF59              ;   BITCI - BIT COUNT IN
01991  EF59              ;   RINONE - FLAG FOR START BIT CHECK <>0 START BIT
01992  EF59              ;   RIDATA - BYTE INPUT BUFFER
01993  EF59              ;   RIPRTY - HOLDS BYTE INPUT PARITY
01994  EF59              ;   RIBUF - INDIRECT POINTER TO DATA BUFFER
01995  EF59              ;   RIDBE - INPUT BUFFER INDEX TO END
01996  EF59              ;   RIDBS - INPUT BUFFER POINTER TO START
01997  EF59              ;   IF RIDBE=RIDBS THEN INPUT BUFFER EMPTY
01998  EF59              ;
01999  EF59  A6 A9       RSRCVR LDX RINONE      ;CHECK FOR START BIT
02000  EF5B  D0 33              BNE RSRTRT      ;WAS START BIT
02001  EF5D              ;

02003  EF5F  F0 36              BEQ RSR030      ;HAVE A FULL BYTE

02005  EF63              ;
02006  EF63              ; CALC PARITY
02007  EF63              ;

02016  EF6D              ;
02017  EF6D              ; EXIT
02018  EF6D              ;
02019  EF6D  60          RSREXT RTS

LINE# LOC   CODE        LINE


02320  F13E              ;***************************************
02321  F13E              ;* GETIN -- GET CHARACTER FROM CHANNEL *
02322  F13E              ;*      CHANNEL IS DETERMINED BY DFLTN.*
02323  F13E              ;* IF DEVICE IS 0, KEYBOARD QUEUE IS   *
02324  F13E              ;* EXAMINED AND A CHARACTER REMOVED IF *
02325  F13E              ;* AVAILABLE.  IF QUEUE IS EMPTY, Z    *
02326  F13E              ;* FLAG IS RETURNED SET.  DEVICES 1-31 *
02327  F13E              ;* ADVANCE TO BASIN.                   *
02328  F13E              ;***************************************
02329  F13E              ;
02330  F13E  A5 99       NGETIN LDA DFLTN       ;CHECK DEVICE
02331  F140  D0 08              BNE GN10        ;NOT KEYBOARD
02332  F142              ;
02333  F142  A5 C6              LDA NDX         ;QUEUE INDEX
02334  F144  F0 0F              BEQ GN20        ;NOBODY THERE...EXIT
02335  F146              ;
02336  F146  78                 SEI
02337  F147  4C B4 E5           JMP LP2         ;GO REMOVE A CHARACTER
02338  F14A              ;
02339  F14A  C9 02       GN10   CMP #2          ;IS IT RS-232
02340  F14C  D0 18              BNE BN10        ;NO...USE BASIN

02342  F14E  84 97       GN232  STY XSAV        ;SAVE .Y, USED IN RS232
02343  F150  20 86 F0           JSR BSI232
02344  F153  A4 97              LDY XSAV        ;RESTORE .Y
02345  F155  18          GN20   CLC             ;GOOD RETURN
02346  F156  60                 RTS



02348  F157              ;***************************************
02349  F157              ;* BASIN-- INPUT CHARACTER FROM CHANNEL*
02350  F157              ;*     INPUT DIFFERS FROM GET ON DEVICE*
02351  F157              ;* #0 FUNCTION WHICH IS KEYBOARD. THE  *
02352  F157              ;* SCREEN EDITOR MAKES READY AN ENTIRE *
02353  F157              ;* LINE WHICH IS PASSED CHAR BY CHAR   *
02354  F157              ;* UP TO THE CARRIAGE RETURN.  OTHER   *
02355  F157              ;* DEVICES ARE:                        *
02356  F157              ;*      0 -- KEYBOARD                  *
02357  F157              ;*      1 -- CASSETTE #1               *
02358  F157              ;*      2 -- RS232                     *
02359  F157              ;*      3 -- SCREEN                    *
02360  F157              ;*   4-31 -- SERIAL BUS                *
02361  F157              ;***************************************
02362  F157              ;
02363  F157  A5 99       NBASIN LDA DFLTN       ;CHECK DEVICE
02364  F159  D0 0B              BNE BN10        ;IS NOT KEYBOARD...
02365  F15B              ;
02366  F15B              ;INPUT FROM KEYBOARD
02367  F15B              ;
02368  F15B  A5 D3              LDA PNTR        ;SAVE CURRENT...
02369  F15D  85 CA              STA LSTP        ;... CURSOR COLUMN
02370  F15F  A5 D6              LDA TBLX        ;SAVE CURRENT...
02371  F161  85 C9              STA LSXP        ;... LINE NUMBER
02372  F163  4C 32 E6           JMP LOOP5       ;BLINK CURSOR UNTIL RETURN

02526  F20E              ;***************************************
02527  F20E              ;* CHKIN -- OPEN CHANNEL FOR INPUT     *
02528  F20E              ;*                                     *
02529  F20E              ;* THE NUMBER OF THE LOGICAL FILE TO BE*
02530  F20E              ;* OPENED FOR INPUT IS PASSED IN .X.   *
02531  F20E              ;* CHKIN SEARCHES THE LOGICAL FILE     *
02532  F20E              ;* TO LOOK UP DEVICE AND COMMAND INFO. *
02533  F20E              ;* ERRORS ARE REPORTED IF THE DEVICE   *
02534  F20E              ;* WAS NOT OPENED FOR INPUT ,(E.G.     *
02535  F20E              ;* CASSETTE WRITE FILE), OR THE LOGICAL*
02536  F20E              ;* FILE HAS NO REFERENCE IN THE TABLES.*
02537  F20E              ;* DEVICE 0, (KEYBOARD), AND DEVICE 3  *
02538  F20E              ;* (SCREEN), REQUIRE NO TABLE ENTRIES  *
02539  F20E              ;* AND ARE HANDLED SEPARATE.           *
02540  F20E              ;***************************************
02541  F20E              ;

02548  F219              ;
02549  F219  A5 BA              LDA FA
02550  F21B  F0 16              BEQ JX320       ;IS KEYBOARD...DONE.
02551  F21D              ;
02552  F21D              ;COULD BE SCREEN, KEYBOARD, OR SERIAL
02553  F21D              ;
02554  F21D  C9 03              CMP #3
02555  F21F  F0 12              BEQ JX320       ;IS SCREEN...DONE.

02662  F291              ;***************************************
02663  F291              ;* CLOSE -- CLOSE LOGICAL FILE       *
02664  F291              ;*                                   *
02665  F291              ;*     THE LOGICAL FILE NUMBER OF THE*
02666  F291              ;* FILE TO BE CLOSED IS PASSED IN .A.*
02667  F291              ;* KEYBOARD, SCREEN, AND FILES NOT   *
02668  F291              ;* OPEN PASS STRAIGHT THROUGH. TAPE  *
02669  F291              ;* FILES OPEN FOR WRITE ARE CLOSED BY*
02670  F291              ;* DUMPING THE LAST BUFFER AND       *
02671  F291              ;* CONDITIONALLY WRITING AN END OF   *
02672  F291              ;* TAPE BLOCK.SERIAL FILES ARE CLOSED*
02673  F291              ;* BY SENDING A CLOSE FILE COMMAND IF*
02674  F291              ;* A SECONDARY ADDRESS WAS SPECIFIED *
02675  F291              ;* IN ITS OPEN COMMAND.              *
02676  F291              ;***************************************
02677  F291              ;

02681  F297  60                 RTS
02682  F298              ;

02809  F333              ;*   UNLISTEN OR UNTALK IEEE DEVICES, BUT   *
02810  F333              ;* LEAVE OTHERS ALONE.  DEFAULT CHANNELS    *
02811  F333              ;* ARE RESTORED.                            *
02812  F333              ;********************************************

02822  F340              ;

02829  F345  A9 00              LDA #0

02991  F409              ; OPN232 - OPEN AN RS-232 OR PARALLEL PORT FILE
02992  F409              ;
02993  F409              ; VARIABLES INITILIZED
02994  F409              ;   BITNUM - # OF BITS TO BE SENT CALC FROM M51CTR
02995  F409              ;   BAUDOF - BAUD RATE FULL
02996  F409              ;   RSSTAT - RS-232 STATUS REG
02997  F409              ;   M51CTR - 6551 CONTROL REG
02998  F409              ;   M51CDR - 6551 COMMAND REG
02999  F409              ;   M51AJB - USER BAUD RATE (CLOCK/BAUD/2-100)
03000  F409              ;   ENABL  - 6526 NMI ENABLES (1-NMI BIT ON)
03001  F409              ;
03002  F409  20 83 F4    OPN232 JSR CLN232      ;SET UP RS232, .Y=0 ON RETURN
03003  F40C              ;
03004  F40C              ; PASS PRAMS TO M51REGS
03005  F40C              ;
03006  F40C  8C 97 02           STY RSSTAT      ;CLEAR STATUS
03007  F40F              ;
03008  F40F  C4 B7       OPN020 CPY FNLEN       ;CHECK IF AT END OF FILENAME
03009  F411  F0 0A              BEQ OPN025      ;YES...
03010  F413              ;
03011  F413  B1 BB              LDA (FNADR)Y    ;MOVE DATA
03012  F415  99 93 02           STA M51CTR,Y    ;TO M51REGS
03013  F418  C8                 INY
03014  F419  C0 04              CPY #4          ;ONLY 4 POSSIBLE PRAMS
03015  F41B  D0 F2              BNE OPN020
03016  F41D              ;
03017  F41D              ; CALC # OF BITS
03018  F41D              ;
03019  F41D  20 4A EF    OPN025 JSR BITCNT
03020  F420  8E 98 02           STX BITNUM
03021  F423              ;
03022  F423              ; CALC BAUD RATE
03023  F423              ;
03024  F423  AD 93 02           LDA M51CTR
03025  F426  29 0F              AND #$0F
03026  F428  F0 1C              BEQ OPN028
03027  F42A              ;
03028  F42A              ; CALCULATE START-TEST RATE...
03029  F42A              ;  DIFFERENT THAN ORIGINAL RELEASE 901227-01
03030  F42A              ;
03031  F42A  0A                 ASL A           ;GET OFFSET INTO TABLES
03032  F42B  AA                 TAX
03033  F42C  AD A6 02           LDA PALNTS      ;GET TV STANDARD
03034  F42F  D0 09              BNE OPN026

03036  F434  BD C0 FE           LDA BAUDO-2,X
03037  F437  4C 40 F4           JMP OPN027

03040  F43D  BD EA E4           LDA BAUDOP-2,X

TIME FUNCTION......PAGE 0056

LINE# LOC   CODE        LINE


03449  F69B              ;***********************************
03450  F69B              ;*                                 *
03451  F69B              ;* TIME                            *
03452  F69B              ;*                                 *
03453  F69B              ;*CONSISTS OF THREE FUNCTIONS:     *
03454  F69B              ;* (1) UDTIM-- UPDATE TIME. USUALLY*
03455  F69B              ;*     CALLED EVERY 60TH SECOND.   *
03456  F69B              ;* (2) SETTIM-- SET TIME. .Y=MSD,  *
03457  F69B              ;*     .X=NEXT SIGNIFICANT,.A=LSD  *
03458  F69B              ;* (3) RDTIM-- READ TIME. .Y=MSD,  *
03459  F69B              ;*     .X=NEXT SIGNIFICANT,.A=LSD  *
03460  F69B              ;*                                 *
03461  F69B              ;***********************************

03463  F69B              ;INTERRUPTS ARE COMING FROM THE 6526 TIMERS
03464  F69B              ;

03466  F69D              ;
03467  F69D              ;HERE WE PROCEED WITH AN INCREMENT
03468  F69D              ;OF THE TIME REGISTER.
03469  F69D              ;

03471  F69F  D0 06              BNE UD30

03474  F6A5  E6 A0              INC TIME
03475  F6A7              ;
03476  F6A7              ;HERE WE CHECK FOR ROLL-OVER 23:59:59
03477  F6A7              ;AND RESET THE CLOCK TO ZERO IF TRUE
03478  F6A7              ;

03480  F6A8  A5 A2              LDA TIME+2

03488  F6B6              ;TIME HAS ROLLED--ZERO REGISTER
03489  F6B6              ;

03492  F6BA  86 A2              STX TIME+2

03503  F6CC  AE 01 DC    UD70   LDX ROWS        ;WAIT TO SETTLE...

CASSETTE READ......PAGE 0062

LINE# LOC   CODE        LINE


03972  F92C              ; VARIABLES USED IN CASSETTE READ ROUTINES
03973  F92C              ;
03974  F92C              ;  REZ - COUNTS ZEROS (IF Z THEN CORRECT # OF DIPOLES)
03975  F92C              ;  RER - FLAGS ERRORS (IF Z THEN NO ERROR)
03976  F92C              ;  DIFF - USED TO PRESERVE SYNO (OUTSIDE OF BIT ROUTINES)
03977  F92C              ;  SYNO - FLAGS IF WE HAVE BLOCK SYNC (16 ZERO DIPOLES)
03978  F92C              ;  SNSW1 - FLAGS IF WE HAVE BYTE SYNC (A LONGLONG)
03979  F92C              ;  DATA - HOLDS MOST RECENT DIPOLE BIT VALUE
03980  F92C              ;  MYCH - HOLDS INPUT BYTE BEING BUILT
03981  F92C              ;  FIRT - USED TO INDICATE WHICH HALF OF DIPOLE WE'RE IN
03982  F92C              ;  SVXT - TEMP USED TO ADJUST SOFTWARE SERVO
03983  F92C              ;  TEMP - USED TO HOLD DIPOLE TIME DURING TYPE CALCULATIONS
03984  F92C              ;  PRTY - HOLDS CURRENT CALCULATED PARITY BIT
03985  F92C              ;  PRP - HAS COMBINED ERROR VALUES FROM BIT ROUTINES
03986  F92C              ;  FSBLK - INDICATE WHICH BLOCK WE'RE LOOKING AT (0 TO EXIT)
03987  F92C              ;  SHCNL - HOLDS FSBLK, USED TO DIRECT ROUTINES, BECAUSE OF EXIT CASE
03988  F92C              ;  RDFLG - HOLDS FUNCTION MODE
03989  F92C              ;     MI - WAITING FOR BLOCK SYNC
03990  F92C              ;     VS - IN DATA BLOCK READING DATA
03991  F92C              ;     NE - WAITING FOR BYTE SYNC
03992  F92C              ;  SAL - INDIRECT TO DATA STORAGE AREA
03993  F92C              ;  SHCNH - LEFT OVER FROM DEBUGGING
03994  F92C              ;  BAD - STORAGE SPACE FOR BAD READ LOCATIONS (BOTTOM OF STACK)
03995  F92C              ;  PTR1 - COUNT OF READ LOCATIONS IN ERROR (POINTER INTO BAD, MAX 61)
03996  F92C              ;  PTR2 - COUNT OF RE-READ LOCATIONS (POINTER INTO BAD, DURING RE-READ)
03997  F92C              ;  VERCHK - VERIFY OR LOAD FLAG (Z - LOADING)
03998  F92C              ;  CMP0 - SOFTWARE SERVO (+/- ADJUST TO TIME CALCS)
03999  F92C              ;  DPSW - IF NZ THEN EXPECTING LL/L COMBINATION THAT ENDS A BYTE
04000  F92C              ;  PCNTR - COUNTS DOWN FROM 8-0 FOR DATA THEN TO FF FOR PARITY
04001  F92C              ;  STUPID - HOLD INDICATOR (NZ - NO T1IRQ YET) FOR T1IRQ
04002  F92C              ;  KIKA26 - HOLDS OLD D1ICR AFTER CLEAR ON READ
04003  F92C              ;

BYTE HANDLER......PAGE 0067

LINE# LOC   CODE        LINE


04178  FA70              ;*************************************************
04179  FA70              ;* BYTE HANDLER OF CASSETTE READ                 *
04180  FA70              ;*                                               *
04181  FA70              ;* THIS PORTION OF IN LINE CODE IS PASSED THE    *
04182  FA70              ;* BYTE ASSEMBLED FROM READING TAPE IN OCHAR.    *
04183  FA70              ;* RER IS SET IF THE BYTE READ IS IN ERROR.      *
04184  FA70              ;* REZ IS SET IF THE INTERRUPT PROGRAM IS READING*
04185  FA70              ;* ZEROS.  RDFLG TELLS US WHAT WE ARE DOING.     *
04186  FA70              ;* BIT 7 SAYS TO IGNORE BYTES UNTIL REZ IS SET   *
04187  FA70              ;* BIT 6 SAYS TO LOAD THE BYTE. OTHERWISE RDFLG  *
04188  FA70              ;* IS A COUNTDOWN AFTER SYNC.  IF VERCK IS SET   *
04189  FA70              ;* WE DO A COMPARE INSTEAD OF A STORE AND SET    *
04190  FA70              ;* STATUS.  FSBLK COUNTS THE TWO BLOCKS. PTR1 IS *
04191  FA70              ;* INDEX TO ERROR TABLE FOR PASS1.  PTR2 IS INDEX*
04192  FA70              ;* TO CORRECTION TABLE FOR PASS2.                *
04193  FA70              ;*************************************************
04194  FA70              ;
04195  FA70              SPERR=16
04196  FA70              CKERR=32
04197  FA70              SBERR=4
04198  FA70              LBERR=8
04199  FA70              ;
04200  FA70  A9 0F       RD15   LDA #$F
04201  FA72              ;
04202  FA72  24 AA              BIT RDFLG       ;TEST FUNCTION MODE
04203  FA74  10 17              BPL RD20        ;NOT WAITING FOR ZEROS
04204  FA76              ;
04205  FA76  A5 B5              LDA DIFF        ;ZEROS YET?
04206  FA78  D0 0C              BNE RD12        ;YES...WAIT FOR SYNC
04207  FA7A  A6 BE              LDX FSBLK       ;IS PASS OVER?
04208  FA7C  CA                 DEX             ;...IF FSBLK ZERO THEN NO ERROR (FIRST GOOD)
04209  FA7D  D0 0B              BNE RD10        ;NO...
04210  FA7F              ;
04211  FA7F  A9 08              LDA #LBERR
04212  FA81  20 1C FE           JSR UDST        ;YES...LONG BLOCK ERROR
04213  FA84  D0 04              BNE RD10        ;BRANCH ALWAYS
04214  FA86              ;
04215  FA86  A9 00       RD12   LDA #0
04216  FA88  85 AA              STA RDFLG       ;NEW MODE IS WAIT FOR SYNC
04217  FA8A  4C BC FE    RD10   JMP PREND       ;EXIT...DONE
04218  FA8D              ;
04219  FA8D  70 31       RD20   BVS RD60        ;WE ARE LOADING
04220  FA8F  D0 18              BNE RD200       ;WE ARE SYNCING
04221  FA91              ;
04222  FA91  A5 B5              LDA DIFF        ;DO WE HAVE BLOCK SYNC...
04223  FA93  D0 F5              BNE RD10        ;...YES, EXIT
04224  FA95  A5 B6              LDA PRP         ;IF FIRST BYTE HAS ERROR...
04225  FA97  D0 F1              BNE RD10        ;...THEN SKIP (EXIT)
04226  FA99  A5 A7              LDA SHCNL       ;MOVE FSBLK TO CARRY...
04227  FA9B  4A                 LSR A
04228  FA9C  A5 BD              LDA OCHAR       ; SHOULD BE A HEADER COUNT CHAR
04229  FA9E  30 03              BMI RD22        ;IF NEG THEN FIRSTBLOCK DATA
04230  FAA0  90 18              BCC RD40        ;...EXPECTING FIRSTBLOCK DATA...YES
04231  FAA2  18                 CLC
04232  FAA3  B0 15       RD22   BCS RD40        ;EXPECTING SECOND BLOCK?...YES
